ReflowInput::ApplyMinMaxBSize().\n *       Similarly, there is ReflowInput::ApplyMinMaxISize() for clamping an\n *       inline-size.\n * @see https://www.w3.org/TR/CSS22/visudet.html#min-max-widths\n * @see https://www.w3.org/TR/CSS22/visudet.html#min-max-heights\n */\ntemplate <class NumericType>\nNumericType CSSMinMax(NumericType aValue, NumericType aMinValue,\n                      NumericType aMaxValue) {\n  NumericType result = aValue;\n  if (aMaxValue < result) {\n    result = aMaxValue;\n  }\n  if (aMinValue > result) {\n    result = aMinValue;\n  }\n  return result;\n}\n\n// A base mAnchorPosResolutionCache = nullptr;\n\n  nsMargin ComputedPhysicalMargin() const {\n    return mComputedMargin.GetPhysicalMargin(mWritingMode);\n  }\n  nsMargin ComputedPhysicalBorderPadding() const {\n    return mComputedBorderPadding.GetPhysicalMargin(mWritingMode);\n  }\n  nsMargin ComputedPhysicalBorder() const {\n    return ComputedLogicalBorder(mWritingMode).GetPhysicalMargin(mWritingMode);\n  }\n  nsMargin ComputedPhysicalPadding() const {\n    return mComputedPadding.GetPhysicalMargin(mWritingMode);\n  }\n\n return mComputedBorderPadding.ConvertTo(aWM, mWritingMode);\n  }\n  LogicalMargin ComputedLogicalPadding(WritingMode aWM) const {\n    return mComputedPadding.ConvertTo(aWM, mWritingMode);\n  }\n  LogicalMargin ComputedLogicalBorder(WritingMode aWM) const {\n    return (mComputedBorderPadding - mComputedPadding)\n        .ConvertTo(aWM, mWritingMode);\n  }\n","numLines":100,"startLine":1,"totalLines":987}}}

implemented across multiple coordinated C++ modules in the layout directory:\\n\\n## Frame Construction\\nFrame construction is implemented in layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.h/cpp, which contains the nsCSSFrameConstructor class responsible for building the frame tree from the DOM. This module constructs frames based on computed styles and manages frame creation for both normal and anonymous content.\\n\\n## Block Layout Reflow\\nBlock layout reflow is implemented through several interconnected modules:\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.h/cpp: The nsBlockFrame class implements block-level layout, handling the reflow of block-level content including proper handling of margins, padding, borders, and child frames.\\n- layout/generic/BlockReflowState.h/cpp: The BlockReflowState class maintains state during block reflow, tracking float management, line layout, and vertical positioning.\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.h/cpp: The nsBlockReflowContext helper class manages the reflow of a single block within its parent container.\\n\\n## Reflow Infrastructure\\nThe reflow pipeline uses data structures defined in:\\n- layout/generic/ReflowInput.h/cpp: Contains the ReflowInput struct that provides input parameters to the Reflow() method, including available space, margin/padding/border calculations, and other sizing parameters.\\n- layout/generic/ReflowOutput.h/cpp: Contains the ReflowOutput struct that receives the output from Reflow(), including desired size and overflow information.\\n\\n## Base Frame Classes and Hierarchy\\nThe frame hierarchy is defined in:\\n- layout/generic/nsIFrame.h/cpp: The nsIFrame interface is the base class for all frames, defining the core Reflow() method signature and invalidation mechanisms.\\n- layout/generic/nsContainerFrame.h/cpp: Container frames that hold child frames, providing the base implementation for frames with children.\\n- layout/generic/nsSplittableFrame.h/cpp: Frames that can be split across pages or columns.\\n\\n## Inline Layout Reflow\\nInline layout is implemented in:\\n- layout/generic/nsLineLayout.h/cpp: Handles inline layout and line breaking for inline content.\\n- layout/generic/nsInlineFrame.h/cpp: The nsInlineFrame class represents inline-level boxes.\\n- layout/generic/nsLineBox.h/cpp: Represents a single line of inline content within a block.\\n\\n## Float Management\\n- layout/generic/nsFloatManager.h/cpp: Manages float positioning and the interaction of floats with other content.\\n\\n## Dirty Frame Invalidation Mechanism\\nThe dirty frame invalidation system tracks which frames need reflow:\\n- layout/base/PresShell.h/cpp: The PresShell class is the main presentation shell that coordinates layout. It contains the FrameNeedsReflow() method that marks frames as needing reflow and manages the reflow process.\\n- layout/base/DepthOrderedFrameList.h/cpp: The DepthOrderedFrameList class maintains a depth-ordered list of dirty frames, enabling efficient processing of frames requiring reflow. It implements the dirty frame tracking list used by PresShell.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameStateBits.h: Defines the frame state bits including NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY and NS_FRAME_HAS_INVALID_RECT that mark frames needing reflow.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameState.h/cpp: Frame state management.\\n\\n## Frame Tree Management\\n- layout/base/nsFrameManager.h/cpp: The nsFrameManager class owns and manages the frame tree, handling frame insertion, removal, and tree structural operations.\\n- layout/base/nsPresContext.h/cpp: The presentation context manages presentation state and links to the frame manager and style system.\\n- layout/base/nsLayoutUtils.h/cpp: Layout utilities used throughout the reflow system.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameList.h/cpp: Frame list management for maintaining lists of frames.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":70,"cache_creation_input_tokens":599,"cache_read_input_tokens":58348,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":599},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7840d673-e518-49aa-a235-02d9f6285563","uuid":"ea5dd7dc-48a9-47c1-ad66-554d1a00cef7"}

implemented across multiple coordinated C++ modules in the layout directory:\\n\\n## Frame Construction\\nFrame construction is implemented in layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.h/cpp, which contains the nsCSSFrameConstructor class responsible for building the frame tree from the DOM. This module constructs frames based on computed styles and manages frame creation for both normal and anonymous content.\\n\\n## Block Layout Reflow\\nBlock layout reflow is implemented through several interconnected modules:\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.h/cpp: The nsBlockFrame class implements block-level layout, handling the reflow of block-level content including proper handling of margins, padding, borders, and child frames.\\n- layout/generic/BlockReflowState.h/cpp: The BlockReflowState class maintains state during block reflow, tracking float management, line layout, and vertical positioning.\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.h/cpp: The nsBlockReflowContext helper class manages the reflow of a single block within its parent container.\\n\\n## Reflow Infrastructure\\nThe reflow pipeline uses data structures defined in:\\n- layout/generic/ReflowInput.h/cpp: Contains the ReflowInput struct that provides input parameters to the Reflow() method, including available space, margin/padding/border calculations, and other sizing parameters.\\n- layout/generic/ReflowOutput.h/cpp: Contains the ReflowOutput struct that receives the output from Reflow(), including desired size and overflow information.\\n\\n## Base Frame Classes and Hierarchy\\nThe frame hierarchy is defined in:\\n- layout/generic/nsIFrame.h/cpp: The nsIFrame interface is the base class for all frames, defining the core Reflow() method signature and invalidation mechanisms.\\n- layout/generic/nsContainerFrame.h/cpp: Container frames that hold child frames, providing the base implementation for frames with children.\\n- layout/generic/nsSplittableFrame.h/cpp: Frames that can be split across pages or columns.\\n\\n## Inline Layout Reflow\\nInline layout is implemented in:\\n- layout/generic/nsLineLayout.h/cpp: Handles inline layout and line breaking for inline content.\\n- layout/generic/nsInlineFrame.h/cpp: The nsInlineFrame class represents inline-level boxes.\\n- layout/generic/nsLineBox.h/cpp: Represents a single line of inline content within a block.\\n\\n## Float Management\\n- layout/generic/nsFloatManager.h/cpp: Manages float positioning and the interaction of floats with other content.\\n\\n## Dirty Frame Invalidation Mechanism\\nThe dirty frame invalidation system tracks which frames need reflow:\\n- layout/base/PresShell.h/cpp: The PresShell class is the main presentation shell that coordinates layout. It contains the FrameNeedsReflow() method that marks frames as needing reflow and manages the reflow process.\\n- layout/base/DepthOrderedFrameList.h/cpp: The DepthOrderedFrameList class maintains a depth-ordered list of dirty frames, enabling efficient processing of frames requiring reflow. It implements the dirty frame tracking list used by PresShell.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameStateBits.h: Defines the frame state bits including NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY and NS_FRAME_HAS_INVALID_RECT that mark frames needing reflow.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameState.h/cpp: Frame state management.\\n\\n## Frame Tree Management\\n- layout/base/nsFrameManager.h/cpp: The nsFrameManager class owns and manages the frame tree, handling frame insertion, removal, and tree structural operations.\\n- layout/base/nsPresContext.h/cpp: The presentation context manages presentation state and links to the frame manager and style system.\\n- layout/base/nsLayoutUtils.h/cpp: Layout utilities used throughout the reflow system.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameList.h/cpp: Frame list management for maintaining lists of frames.\"\n}\n","numLines":47,"startLine":1,"totalLines":47}}}
